  $('#tab_email').addClass('active');
  $('#tab_menu_email').addClass('active');
});</script><script>$("#subscribe_button_email").click(function (event) {
  event.preventDefault();
  var address = $("#subscribe_email_address").val();
  var email = $("#email").val();
  $.ajax({
    url: '/subscriber/add',
    type: "POST",
    data: ({
      statuspage_id: "564314ae3309c22c3b0002fa",
      method: "email",
      address: address,
      email: email
    }),
    success: function(data){
      var message_text = data.status.message;
      if (message_text == 'OK') {
        message_text = 'Thanks for subscribing. Check your email for instructions.';
      }
      $("#result_subscribe_email").html("<span class=\"help-block\">"+message_text+"</span>");
      $("#result_subscribe_email").show();
      setTimeout(function(){
        $("#result_subscribe_email").fadeOut("slow", function () {
        $("#result_subscribe_email").hide();
            });
      }, 5000);
    }
  });
})
</script><script>$("#subscribe_button_sms").click(function (event) {
  event.preventDefault();
  var address = $("#subscribe_sms_country_code").val() + $("#subscribe_sms_number").val();
  $.ajax({
    url: '/subscriber/add',
    type: "POST",
    data: ({
      statuspage_id: "564314ae3309c22c3b0002fa",
      method: "sms",
      address: address
    }),
    success: function(data){
      var message_text = data.status.message;
      if (message_text == 'OK') {
        message_text = 'Check your phone for the confirmation text message';
      }          
      $("#result_subscribe_sms").html("<span class=\"help-block\">"+message_text+"</span>");
      $("#result_subscribe_sms").show();
      setTimeout(function(){
        $("#result_subscribe_sms").fadeOut("slow", function () {
        $("#result_subscribe_sms").hide();
            });
      }, 8000);
    }
  });
})
</script><script>$("#subscribe_button_webhook").click(function (event) {
  event.preventDefault();
  var address = $("#subscribe_webhook_address").val();
  var address_email = $("#subscribe_webhook_address_email").val();
  $.ajax({
    url: '/subscriber/add',
    type: "POST",
    data: ({
      statuspage_id: "564314ae3309c22c3b0002fa",
      method: "webhook",
      address: address,
      address_email: address_email
    }),
    success: function(data){
      var message_text = data.status.message;
      if (message_text == 'OK') {
        message_text = 'Thanks for subscribing. Check your email for instructions.';
      }          
      $("#result_subscribe_webhook").html("<span class=\"help-block\">"+message_text+"</span>");
      $("#result_subscribe_webhook").show();
      setTimeout(function(){
        $("#result_subscribe_webhook").fadeOut("slow", function () {
        $("#result_subscribe_webhook").hide();
            });
      }, 5000);
    }
  });
})

href="http://capinaremos.com/2017/03/24/capinascreen-5-motivos-pra-voce-comecar-travelers/" rel="bookmark">CapinaScreen: 5 motivos pra você começar Travelers!</a></h1><div id="post-info-wrap" class="left relative"><div class="post-info-out"><div class="post-info-img left relative"> <img alt='' src='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/616080a7827867cdf602795da63234d4?s=50&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' class="post-info-right left relative"><div class="post-info-name left relative" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/Person"> <span class="post-info-text">Por</span> <span class="author-name vcard fn author" itemprop="name"><a href="http://capinaremos.com/author/brunaborni/" title="Posts de Bruna Borni" rel="author">Bruna Borni</a></span></div><div class="post-info-date left relative"> <span class="post-info-text">Publicado em</span> <span class="post-date updated"><time class="post-date updated" itemprop="datePublished" class="post-cont-in"><div class="left relative" id="content-main"><p><strong>Travelers</strong> é uma das séries originais da <strong>Netflix</strong> que o povo não dá muita atenção. Comecei a assistir dando um tiro no escuro, a primeira impressão foi horrível, mas felizmente(ou infelizmente) eu tenho a péssima mania de assistir até o final, mesmo que ache a série ou filme uma bosta. É um terrível fardo a se carregar, tive que assitir Fuller House até o final, mas no caso de Travelers não foi um absoluto tempo perdido.</p><p><img data-attachment-id="57356" data-permalink="http://capinaremos.com/2017/03/24/capinascreen-5-motivos-pra-voce-comecar-travelers/images-4/" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/capinaremos.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/2/2017/03/images.jpg?fit=300%2C168" data-orig-size="300,168" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="images" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/capinaremos.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/2/2017/03/images.jpg?fit=300%2C168" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/capinaremos.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/2/2017/03/images.jpg?fit=300%2C168" class="aligncenter wp-image-57356" src="https://i2.wp.com/capinaremos.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/2/2017/03/images.jpg?resize=554%2C310" alt="" data-recalc-dims="1" /></p><p>Bem, a série é e não é ficção científica. O tempo da série não é o futuro, como The Expanse, mas sim o presente. Os viajantes do tempo vem para o nosso século a fim de modificar o futuro apocalíptico, recebendo missões de um programador/presidente do mundo/deus na terra fodão do futuro.</p><p>Leia mais sobre a série no post de hoje amigão!</p><p><a class="more-link" href="http://capinaremos.com/2017/03/24/capinascreen-5-motivos-pra-voce-comecar-travelers/"><span>Continue Lendo</span></a></p><div
